# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
The gradient represent the increase in cost for
every increase in 1 person ^UTZnhAu0

The gradient represent the decrease in price for every extra kg
of sand bought ^h09B5ffV

There is no x intercept because
there is a minimal cost.
The y intercept represent the minumum
cost to rent the room even for
0 persons ^d8fkJ0DK

There is no x or y intercept,
at y intercept the quantity would have
to be 0 which is not possible
and at x intercept the price
would have to be 0 ^pbYxhnRQ
